             <h4 class="c-education-sector-item__title">
              CoderDojo
             </h4>
             <p class="c-education-sector-item__caption">
              CoderDojos are free, creative coding clubs in community spaces for young people aged 717
             </p>
            </a>
           </li>
           <li class="c-education-sector__item">
            <a class="c-education-sector-item" href="https://www.raspberrypi.org/jam/">
             <div class="o-media o-media--top">

               <img alt="Raspberry Jams" class="c-education-sector-item__image" src="/homepage-9df4b/static/raspberry-jam-e87aa2f14d635d4b4384cd284b4c51a0.png"/>
              </div>
              <div class="o-media__fluid">
               <h4 class="c-education-sector-item__title">
                Raspberry Jams

     <section class="c-home-mission">
      <div class="o-container">
       <h2 class="c-home-mission__title">
        <span class="u-visually-hidden">
         Our Mission
        </span>
       </h2>
       <div class="o-grid o-grid--center">
        <div class="o-grid__col u-8/12@sm u-7/12@lg">
         <p class="c-home-mission__content">
          Our mission is to put the power of computing and digital making into the hands of people all over the world. We do this so that more people are able to harness the power of computing and digital technologies for work, to solve problems that matter to them, and to express themselves creatively.
         </p>
         <p class="c-home-mission__cta">
          <a class="c-home-mission__link" href="/donate/">
           Donate to support our work
          </a>
         </p>
        </div>
